 3485|       |                            wasm_set_exception(module,
 3486|       |                                               "out of bounds array access");
 3487|       |                            goto got_exception;
 3488|       |                        }
 3489|       |
 3490|       |                        if (opcode == WASM_OP_STRING_ENCODE_WTF16_ARRAY) {
 3491|       |                            if (array_type->elem_type != VALUE_TYPE_I16) {
 3492|       |                                wasm_set_exception(module,
 3493|       |                                                   "array type mismatch");
 3494|       |                                goto got_exception;
 3495|       |                            }
 3496|       |                            flag = WTF16;
 3497|       |                        }
 3498|       |                        else {
 3499|       |                            if (array_type->elem_type != VALUE_TYPE_I8) {
 3500|       |                                wasm_set_exception(module,
 3501|       |                                                   "array type mismatch");
 3502|       |                                goto got_exception;
 3503|       |                            }
 3504|       |                            if (opcode == WASM_OP_STRING_ENCODE_UTF8_ARRAY) {
 3505|       |                                flag = UTF8;
 3506|       |                            }
 3507|       |                            else if (opcode
 3508|       |                                     == WASM_OP_STRING_ENCODE_WTF8_ARRAY) {
 3509|       |                                flag = WTF8;
 3510|       |                            }
 3511|       |                            else if (
 3512|       |                                opcode
 3513|       |                                == WASM_OP_STRING_ENCODE_LOSSY_UTF8_ARRAY) {
 3514|       |                                flag = LOSSY_UTF8;
 3515|       |                            }
 3516|       |                        }

 3518|       |                        count = wasm_string_measure(str_obj, flag);
 3519|       |
 3520|       |                        bytes_written = wasm_string_encode(
 3521|       |                            str_obj, 0, count, arr_start_addr, NULL, flag);
 3522|       |
 3523|       |                        if (bytes_written < 0) {
 3524|       |                            if (bytes_written == Isolated_Surrogate) {
 3525|       |                                wasm_set_exception(
 3526|       |                                    module, "isolated surrogate is seen");
 3527|       |                            }

 3529|       |                                wasm_set_exception(
 3530|       |                                    module, "array space is insufficient");
 3531|       |                            }
 3532|       |                            else {
 3533|       |                                wasm_set_exception(module, "encode failed");
 3534|       |                            }
 3535|       |
 3536|       |                            goto got_exception;
 3537|       |                        }
 3538|       |
 3539|       |                        PUSH_I32(bytes_written);
 3540|       |                        HANDLE_OP_END();
 3541|       |                    }
 3542|       |#endif /* end of WASM_ENABLE_STRINGREF != 0 */

 3547|      0|                        goto got_exception;
 3548|      0|                    }
 3549|      0|                }
